These are exported as recognized/unsupported findings only; the browser runtime does not render IKEMEN model scenes or decode video-backed backgrounds.
- `pnpm qa:trace` writes `diagnostics.json.coverage`, a compact machine-readable coverage matrix across controller families, typed operations, effect kinds, combat reasons, match-pause advance/freeze routes, world lifecycle routes, target-link routes, and effect-store routes. The command fails if required critical-spine coverage disappears for `hitdef`, `kinematic:velset`, `kinematic:veladd`, `kinematic:velmul`, `kinematic:posset`, `kinematic:posadd`, `kinematic:gravity`, `kinematic:hitvelset`, `resource:lifeadd`, `resource:lifeset`, `resource:poweradd`, `resource:powerset`, `bounds:posfreeze`, `bounds:screenbound`, `collision:width`, `collision:playerpush`, `metadata:statetypeset`, `orientation:turn`, `sprite-effect:trans`, `sprite-effect:sprpriority`, sprite-effect, target, pause, projectile/helper/explod, reversal, damage-scale, resource, required imported runtime artifacts, and bounded HitPause/Pause/SuperPause advance/freeze routes. The current critical artifact spine includes `synthetic-imported-trans-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-sprpriority-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-lifeadd-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-resourceset-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-control-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-screenbound-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-posfreeze-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-playerpush-dynamic`, `synthetic-imported-width-dynamic`, and the previous required controller/runtime oracles listed in the trace gate registry.
- `pnpm qa:trace` also requires `synthetic-imported-dynamic-posadd` and `synthetic-imported-dynamic-posset` in the critical-spine coverage contract so bounded active-state dynamic position typed telemetry cannot silently disappear from the required artifact set.
- `pnpm qa:trace` also requires `synthetic-imported-controller-param-root-redirect`, `synthetic-imported-helper-controller-param-parentroot`, `synthetic-imported-helper-dynamic-veladd`, `synthetic-imported-controller-param-target-redirect`, `synthetic-imported-controller-param-bottom`, `synthetic-imported-target-cond-bottom`, and `synthetic-imported-target-ifelse-bottom` in the coverage contract so bounded controller-param Root redirect, helper-local controller-param Parent/Root redirect, helper-local dynamic VelAdd redirect, Target redirect, controller-param bottom fallback, `Cond(...)` lazy bottom isolation, and `IfElse(...)` returned-branch bottom isolation oracles cannot silently disappear from the required artifact set.

## Current Explod RemoveOnGetHit Cut

- `Explod` now carries bounded `removeongethit` data through compiled `ExplodControllerOp` and raw controller fallback.
- `RuntimeEffectActorWorld` can prune owner-side Explods flagged with `removeongethit = 1` when that owner enters the current direct hit/guard or projectile hit/guard routes.
- `synthetic-imported-explod-removeongethit.json` proves a P2-owned flagged Explod spawns, P2 is hit, MatchWorld emits Explod remove lifecycle evidence, and the P2 effect store records the produced serial.
- `synthetic-imported-explod-removeonprojectilehit.json` proves an imported P1 Projectile can hit imported P2, trigger the shared projectile get-hit callback, and prune P2's flagged Explod while preserving projectile lifecycle evidence.
- `synthetic-imported-explod-removeonprojectileguard.json` proves the same owner-side pruning when imported P2 blocks that bounded projectile route.
- This is `executed-partial`: exact MUGEN/IKEMEN tick order, helper-bound Explod cleanup timing beyond the bounded static helper-local remove-id route, custom-state edge cases, FightFX/common animation routing, and broader remove-trigger parity remain unsupported.

## Current Explod Pause-Budget Cut

- `ExplodControllerOp` now carries bounded `ignorehitpause`, `pausemovetime`, and `supermovetime` params through compiled CNS data and raw controller fallback.
- During hit pause, `PlayableMatchRuntime` advances bounded paused-presentation actors with `ignorehitpause = 1` and runs a bounded imported active-state controller pass for controllers marked `ignorehitpause = 1`; it still does not advance full physics/AI/animation.
- During `Pause`/`SuperPause`, source actor `movetime` still advances its effects as before, then paused presentation passes advance only Explods with remaining `pausemovetime`/`supermovetime` budget.
- `synthetic-imported-explod-ignorehitpause.json` proves one P1 Explod freezes during hitpause while a second P1 Explod with `ignorehitpause = 1` continues to advance. Current checksum: `a351168e`.
- `synthetic-imported-hitpausetime-ignorehitpause.json` proves imported P1 can route from active state `200` to `220` during hitpause through `HitPauseTime > 0` on a `ChangeState` marked `ignorehitpause = 1`, while P1 records player advance and P2 records player freeze. Current checksum: `a3a78bb8`.
- `synthetic-imported-explod-pausemovetime.json` proves one P1 Explod freezes during regular `Pause` while a second P1 Explod with `pausemovetime = 4` continues to advance after source `movetime` ends. Current checksum: `467c2030`.
- `synthetic-imported-explod-supermovetime.json` proves the matching bounded route during `SuperPause` with `supermovetime = 4`. Current checksum: `1d99f66f`.
- This is `executed-partial`: exact MUGEN/IKEMEN pause layering, helper-bound Explod pause timing, sound/spark timing, super backgrounds, FightFX/common animation routing, and tick-order parity remain unsupported.

## Current Runtime Presentation Snapshot Cut

- `RuntimeMatchPresentationSnapshotWorld` owns the bounded adapter that builds match presentation snapshot inputs before `RuntimeSnapshotWorld.match()` assembles the final renderer-independent snapshot.
- Camera shake, stage flash, and P1/P2 effect snapshot groups route through this seam instead of being collected inline in `PlayableMatchRuntime.getSnapshot()`.
- Focused `RuntimeMatchPresentationSnapshotSystem` coverage proves shake/flash/effect-group forwarding and P1/P2 ordering.
- This is `executed-partial` ownership only: exact stage/motif camera logic, effect lifecycle semantics, renderer/audio parity, visual/debug UI parity, and full match snapshot parity remain unsupported.

## Current Runtime Active Controller Telemetry Cut

- `RuntimeActiveControllerTelemetryWorld` owns the bounded adapter that builds active-controller telemetry hooks before active state hooks, side-effect dispatchers, and fallback runtime-controller dispatch run.
- The shared hook set forwards controller and typed-operation records into `RuntimeCompatibilityTelemetryWorld`, leaving imported filtering, event keys, retention, and report projection in the telemetry world.
- Focused `RuntimeActiveControllerTelemetrySystem` coverage proves controller and operation forwarding through the seam.
- This is `executed-partial` ownership only: exact telemetry event semantics, imported-only filtering, event retention limits, helper/team/redirect telemetry breadth, visual/debug UI parity, and full CNS VM parity remain unsupported.

## Current Runtime Combat State Hook Cut

- `RuntimeMatchCombatStateHooksWorld` owns the bounded adapter that builds state-entry hooks for direct/projectile combat and helper combat before the match combat bridge runs.
- Direct/projectile combat hooks preserve state-owner availability checks and entry options for owner-backed custom-state routes; helper combat hooks keep self-owned availability checks while still forwarding entry options into the shared state-entry path.
- Focused `RuntimeMatchCombatStateHooksSystem` coverage proves both adapter contracts.
- This is `executed-partial` ownership only: helper-owned custom-state table breadth, throws, teams/simul actor registries, multi-target helper ownership, exact combat/helper tick order, visual/audio parity, and full combat/helper VM parity remain unsupported.

## Current Helper NumEnemy Cut

- `ExpressionEvaluator` can evaluate `NumEnemy` through an explicit provider before falling back to the current one-opponent context.
- `HelperSystem` derives helper-local `NumEnemy` from the nearest-sorted supplied `opponentStates` list, so helper-local CNS can gate `EnemyNear(index)` reads with the same bounded opponent roster used by runtime expression contexts.
- `HelperSystem` can also accept `opponentRoster` entries with id plus runtime state, preserving that metadata through nearest ordering so non-current helper-local `EnemyNear(index), TeamSide` reads can resolve.
- `RuntimeOpponentSelectionWorld` can build id-bearing `opponentRoster` entries in nearest order without cloning runtime states.
- `RuntimeEffectLifecycleWorld` can accept an explicit lifecycle `opponents` list and turn it into an id-bearing nearest-order `opponentRoster` built by `RuntimeOpponentSelectionWorld` for active and paused visual Helper lifecycle contexts, while keeping `opponentId` / `opponentState` for existing fallback paths.
- `RuntimeMatchOpponentContextWorld` owns the concrete 1v1 match/pause/hitpause opponent context source used by `RuntimeMatchInteractionWorld`, `RuntimePausedMatchWorld`, and `RuntimeHitPauseWorld`: P1/P2 mirror into direct opponent plus explicit one-opponent lifecycle list, while actors outside the pair fail closed.
- Focused `RuntimeCnsSubset` coverage proves explicit provider values and invalid-provider clamping, `RuntimeOpponentSelectionSystem` coverage proves id-bearing roster construction, `EffectActorSystem` coverage proves helper-local `NumEnemy = 2` in the same route that reads `EnemyNear(1)`, proves an unsorted `[far, near, tie]` helper-local list resolves by nearest/stable-tie ordering, and proves `EnemyNear(1), TeamSide = 2` against id-bearing roster entries, while `EffectLifecycleSystem` coverage proves active/paused lifecycle roster forwarding and explicit lifecycle opponent-list routing without leaking control fields into helper options. `MatchInteractionSystem`, `PauseSystem`, and `RuntimeHitPauseSystem` coverage proves concrete 1v1 lifecycle calls forward `[current opponent]` plus stage/runtime tick metadata.
- This is `executed-partial`: real team/simul roster ownership, automatic multi-opponent match roster discovery, helper-owned opponent roster discovery, richer identity metadata beyond ids/team side, y-axis/priority selection parity, redirects beyond supplied lists, visual parity, and full Helper trigger parity remain unsupported.

## Current Runtime Opponent Roster Cut

- `RuntimeExpressionContextWorld` can evaluate `EnemyNear(index)` / `EnemyNear(var(n))` and `NumEnemy` through an explicit caller-supplied opponent roster before falling back to the current one-opponent context.
- Explicit rosters are sorted by `RuntimeOpponentSelectionWorld` before `EnemyNear(index)` resolves; stable ties preserve caller order, finite candidates sort before non-finite positions, and `NumEnemy` still reports supplied roster length.

## Current Helper Target Cut

- `HelperSystem` can remember explicit/default/bare direct `HitDef` targets for first-generation visual Helpers, mirror explicit/default helper-parented Projectile contact targets into the spawning Helper, execute bounded Target side effects from direct-HitDef or helper-parented Projectile target memory, and expose target refs in helper snapshots.
- `RuntimeEffectLifecycleWorld` supplies current opponent id/state so helper-local `NumTarget(id)` and `Target(id), Life` can branch only after that helper has remembered P2.

- This is `executed-partial`: bounded helper-owned direct-HitDef and explicit/default helper-parented Projectile `TargetLifeAdd`, `TargetPowerAdd`, `TargetVelSet`, `TargetVelAdd`, `TargetFacing`, `TargetBind`, `TargetDrop`, helper-parented Projectile bare `Target, Life`, plus owner-backed `TargetState`, are trace-gated for remembered targets, but helper-owned custom state tables, teams, multi-target selection, exact lifetime/tick order, and full helper target parity remain unsupported.

## Current Helper NumProj Cut

- `HelperSystem` can evaluate bounded helper-local `NumProj` / `NumProjID(id)` through a callback supplied by `RuntimeEffectActorWorld`.
- `RuntimeEffectActorWorld` counts only owner-side Projectile actors whose `parentId` matches the current Helper runtime serial, and excludes removed Projectiles.
- `synthetic-imported-helper-numproj.json` checksum `3312a554` proves a visual Helper can spawn owner-side Projectile anim `944`, then branch from state `1200` to `1213` / anim `933` through `NumProjID(8851) > 0`.
- Focused `EffectActorSystem` coverage proves same-id player-owned Projectiles do not satisfy the helper-local count and removed helper-parented Projectiles are excluded.
- This is `executed-partial`: helper-owned Projectile combat/contact presentation, exact projectile namespaces/scopes, `ProjContact` timing, dynamic ids beyond gated static/default ids, teams, exact tick order, and full Helper/Projectile trigger parity remain unsupported.

## Current Edge-Distance Expression Cut

- `FrontEdgeDist`, `BackEdgeDist`, `FrontEdgeBodyDist`, and `BackEdgeBodyDist` use current stage bounds when the runtime supplies `{ left, right }`.
- Body variants subtract the current actor `bodyWidth.front` / `bodyWidth.back` and clamp at `0`; missing body width keeps the existing bounded fallback width.
- `PlayableMatchRuntime`, `RuntimeExpressionContextWorld`, `RuntimeControllerEvaluationContextWorld`, `StateControllerExecutor`, extracted passive controller systems, and `HelperSystem` now forward stage bounds into expression evaluation.
- Required `synthetic-imported-edge-distance.json` checksum `785de452` proves an imported State -1 route can branch through `FrontEdgeDist = 340`, `BackEdgeDist = 300`, `FrontEdgeBodyDist = 301`, and `BackEdgeBodyDist = 261` into state/action `293` without combat side effects.
- Focused coverage proves direct evaluator values, active runtime context values, helper-local trigger branches, and helper-local controller expressions. Missing stage bounds still return `999` so partial character loads do not crash.
- This is `executed-partial`: exact camera/screen edge behavior, localcoord scaling, teams/simul, complex helper namespaces, push/corner parity, and full MUGEN/IKEMEN edge-distance parity remain unsupported.

## Current Helper Projectile Cut

- `HelperSystem` can dispatch bounded helper-local static `Projectile` through a callback supplied by `RuntimeEffectActorWorld`.
- `RuntimeEffectActorWorld` spawns that Projectile in the owner-side Projectile store and preserves the Helper runtime serial as `parentId`.
- `synthetic-imported-helper-projectile.json` checksum `b6269136` proves a visual Helper can route from state `1200` to `1212` / anim `932` while spawning owner-side Projectile anim `943` with `parentId = p1-helper-0`.
- This is `executed-partial`: helper-owned Projectile combat/contact presentation, exact projectile namespaces, dynamic params beyond gated static/default ids, exact tick order, and full Helper/Projectile parity remain unsupported.

## Sprite Atlas Pipeline

- `AtlasSpriteProvider` can consume `sprite-atlas-builder` output: `sprite-sheet-alpha.png` plus `manifest.json.frame_layout`.
- `SffSpriteProvider` can consume decoded SFF v1 and SFF v2 archives from the browser loader.
- `CompositeSpriteProvider` routes selected group ranges to atlas-backed characters, supports owner-specific lookups for imported custom-state rendering, and falls back to procedural sprites for unsupported groups.
- Loaded decoded SFF routes take priority for their sprite groups so imported runtime actors can render their own art.
- Default action mapping is prepared for fighting rows: `idle`, `crouch`, `walk-forward`, `jump`, `punch`, `kick`, `hitstun`.
- The imagegen-sheet normalizer uses one character-level reference scale, so crouch/jump frames are not enlarged by independent per-frame fitting.
- Individual rows can be regenerated as new imagegen art and inserted with `scripts/replace_atlas_state_from_imagegen_row.py`; this is the preferred fix for bad locomotion poses over cutting or mechanically repairing old frames.
- The inspector fallback still uses procedural sprites when imported SFF images cannot be decoded.

## Not Supported Yet

- Remaining SFF edge cases: SFF v2.1 PNG paths, truecolor palette behavior, broader palette-bank/source semantics, and malformed or unusual encodings.
- Exact external ACT/SFF palette parity; current `RemapPal` support can apply loaded ACT destination palettes to decoded indexed SFF sprites, but exact source-palette semantics, group/bank ownership, IKEMEN helper/team/redirect ownership, truecolor/PNG remap, and engine-perfect blend order remain partial.
- Full CNS expression language.
- Full state-controller execution beyond the hand-authored playable subset and imported CMD State -1 bridge.
- Remaining CMD timing edge cases: `autogreater`, `buffer.pauseend`, `buffer.shared`, exact charge storage and conflict behavior, and exact MUGEN/IKEMEN input quirks.
- Exact visual/system controller parity for `Pause`/`SuperPause` beyond the extracted `PauseSystem` subset; broader helper/projectile/explod pause rules beyond the current bounded projectile and visual Helper/Explod movetime advance/freeze gates, pause layering, sound/spark timing, super backgrounds, custom states, exact `PosFreeze`/`ScreenBound` parity, exact attr/slot semantics beyond the simplified `CombatResolver` `HitBy`/`NotHitBy` path, exact `AttackMulSet`/`DefenceMulSet` scaling order beyond the bounded direct/projectile damage multiplier path, exact target/custom-state ownership, and exact `HitOverride`/`ReversalDef` parity beyond the current redirect/counter subset.
- Exact `AssertSpecial` parity beyond current `NoWalk`/`NoAutoTurn`/`Invisible`, bounded global-style flag telemetry for `nobardisplay`/`nobg`/`nofg`/`nokosnd`/`nomusic`, bounded official `Intro` / `NoKOSlow` telemetry, bounded shadow presentation handoff for local `noshadow` and global `globalnoshadow` including the current `GlobalNoShadow` helper/explod actor-frame route, bounded `TimerFreeze`, bounded `RoundNotOver` active round-finish hold, bounded stand/crouch/air guard-flag blocking with required guard-deny evidence and minimum flag-before-HitDef order, bounded one-frame trigger-expiry evidence, bounded `NoGetUpFromLieDown`, bounded `NoFastRecoverFromLieDown`, attacker-side `Unguardable`, and defender-side `NoKO` nonlethal damage clamp behavior with minimum flag-before-HitDef order. Broader lifetime persistence/layering, priority, pause interaction, exact intro/KO slow-motion/winpose/lifebar/round-flow effects, HUD hiding, background hiding, KO sound/music behavior, exact shadow skew/stage parameters/layering, projectile shadow semantics, no-KO semantics beyond this clamp, helper/team/global behavior beyond the current spawned helper/explod route, and KFM/Common1 confirmation still need dedicated systems.
- Exact `ChangeAnim2` parity for missing-action fallback, redirects, and multiple simultaneously imported SFF namespaces. The current playable path uses the state owner's action table for owner-backed states and exposes sprite-owner metadata for renderer/debug routing.
